<Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
Great gym, met a climber YouTuber here, the people seem friendly, really safe (strict) with belay test, usual price.

Route setting was amazing for boulders; they also have some cool unique features like a very very huge boulder overhang, archways, and slab walls. I can't imagine getting bored here; has every style of bouldering to please all with an insane amount of different holds.

Grading is little on the soft side, and top rope is ATC. Very spacious and clean. Seriously glad to pick this gym as i only had few days to try two in the area.<//text>

Cliffs is my regular climbing gym. I tried out and actually became a member of sender one before I joined cliffs. My friends got me in on a guest pass and sender was never the same. Very chill atmosphere here, especially during the day. The bouldering is fantastic so you can go alone and have a blast which is great for keeping strong. The lead section is somewhat small but is very fun and thoughtful. I love the routesetting at this gym. Can be a bit crowded starting at like 6:30 - 7 on weekdays so I'd go straight after work, but that's everywhere in Los Angeles. Very active route refreshing. Always feels like there's something new to try but sometimes your project can be removed before you finish it. Sauna and training room above the climbing floor are great as well.

Having said that their policy on "couples membership" is ridiculous. The demand a joint bank account statement or marriage license? We brought in a signed lease with both of our names on it and one of the desk staff treated us very curtly when we thought that seemed reasonable. All to grub for an extra $50 as well. This experience almost soured me on the gym immediately but I'm glad I stuck around.</Text>

I've been to three climbing gyms: Boulderdash in the San Fernando Valley, LA Boulders (a Touchstone gym like Cliffs of Id), and this gym (Cliffs if Id). Cliffs of Id is by far the best.

< Review>
*update 5-1-2019* they added a 4th treadmill but one of them has been broken for a month. So has one of the stationary bikes. One of the showers has been broken for over a month. The staff is indifferent. "Cliffs" is synonymous with disrepair.*/update*

*update 3-22-2018* 2 of the 3 treadmills are out of service, one has been out of service for over a month.*/update*

The walls and routes are nice and offer variety. The climbing is good but there are a few things that majorly detract from this location as a be-all gym.

Parking is a nightmare during peak hours.

Gym equipment is in disrepair (treadmills don't work or go beyond a slow jog, broken mirrors, stuck bench press rack, etc.) And the gym area is cramped and not well equipped.

They also have a debit and credit card minimum which I find inconvenient but the management is dismissive of my opinion. I've just stopped purchasing snacks from here.

Again, the climbing is good but everything else could use some work.<//Review>

< Text>
Gosh. this is seriously harder than it looks!

Ive rocked climb with a harness plenty of times and I guess this was my first REAL experience at bouldering and it beat me up pretty good!

The feeling of a harness obviously makes you feel invincible but the fact that you have no security but a seemingly bouncy floor doesn't make me feel too comfortable climbing all the way up without feeling a bit queasy in the tummy!

I actually don't have a fear of heights until that day, the instructor however did their best on introducing different techniques to help us climb better but it was still a work in progress. Def worth a couple more tries that is for sure!<//Text>

My home climbing gym! Everything you need is here - gym facilities, yoga, bordering, training walls, classes, top rope / sport climbing. They have food trucks on some weeknights. < Review>
Trendiest, cleanest, largest gym I've ever been to. They even have a local coffee shop make a special blend roasted just for their iced coffee they sell in store.

The climbing structures are huge, terrain varied, holds clean, routes well spaced. No autobelays. Expensive, as you would expect. Ratings are very soft so you can be pleased with the ratings you climb here. Overall had a great first time visit, would be a member if I lived closer.

It's a Touchstone gym so I think membership includes some bay area gyms.</Review>

<userid>105426647877382707204<//userid><user_name>brad gardiner<//user_name>< Date>
1541118994025</Date>
<Rate>5</Rate>< review>
For a Subway, this is 5 stars and pretty much the only one I go to any more.

Happy is a sandwich making wizard and rolls the meat so it has air in the middle and doesn't slap it all together like a bologna and potato chip sandwich.

This spot has paper bags for togo orders and not the plastic ones that make my sandwiches taste like they sat in a steam room for a day and a half when I open them up.

They have the bread baking schedule dialed in also.  Always fresh.

Subway isn't my goto restaurant for lunch but this one is good when I have a food emergency or don't want to spend $20 at another fast food place.< /review>
